style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Refining &#38; Marketing (R&#38;M)</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%">Segment adjusted EBITDA was $4.4 billion in the third quarter of 2023, versus $5.5 billion for the third quarter of 2022. Refining &#38; Marketing segment adjusted EBITDA was $16.06 per barrel for the third quarter of 2023, versus $19.87 per barrel for the third quarter of 2022. Segment adjusted EBITDA excludes refining planned turnaround costs, which totaled $153 million in the third quarter of 2023 and $384 million in the third quarter of 2022.</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:115%"> The decrease in segment adjusted EBITDA was driven by lower market crack spreads.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">R&#38;M margin was $26.16 per barrel for the third quarter of 2023, versus $30.21 per b</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">arrel for the third quarter of 2022. Crude capacity utilization was approximately 94%, resulting in total throughput of 3.0 million barrels per day for the third quarter of 2023.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Refining operating costs per barrel were $5.14 for the third quarter of 2023, versus $5.63 for the third quarter of 2022.</font><font style="color:#ee2724;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">This decrease was primarily driven by lower energy costs.</font></div><div id="i577082ea0902489687fa8ebcb7144506_16"></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Midstream</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Segment adjusted EBITDA was $1.5 billion in the third quarter of 2023, versus $1.5 billion for the third quarter of 2022. The results were primarily driven by higher rates, growth from equity affiliates, and higher total throughputs, partially offset by lower natural gas liquids prices.</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> Third-quarter 2023 segment adjusted EBITDA excludes Garyville incident response costs of $63 million.</font></div><div id="i577082ea0902489687fa8ebcb7144506_19"></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Corporate and Items Not Allocated</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Corporate expenses totaled $246 million in the third quarter of 2023, compared with $173 million in the third quarter of 2022. The variance was primarily driven by a $35 million charge related to valuation of existing performance-based stock compensation expense and $25 million of non-operating equipment disposal expense.</font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:6pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt;text-align:right"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">2</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt;text-align:right"><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:72pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">In the third quarter of 2023, items not allocated to segments include a $106 million gain on the sale of the company&#8217;s interest in the South Texas Gateway Terminal. In the third quarter of 2022, items not allocated to segments include a $549 million gain for the contribution of the Martinez assets to the Martinez Renewables LLC joint venture and a $509 million gain related to an MPLX LP (NYSE&#58; MPLX) reclassification of a third-party contract. These have been excluded from the company&#8217;s adjusted results.</font></div><div id="i577082ea0902489687fa8ebcb7144506_22"></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Financial Position, Liquidity, and Return of Capital </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">As of September&#160;30, 2023, MPC had $13.1 billion of cash, cash equivalents, and short-term investments and $5 billion available on its bank revolving credit facility. </font></div><div><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">In the third quarter, the company returned approximately </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">$3.1 billion</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%"> of capital to shareholders through </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">$2.8 billion</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%"> of share repurchases and </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">$297 million</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%"> of dividends. Through October 27, the company repurchased an additional $1.0 billion of company shares. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">On October 25, MPC announced that its Board of Directors approved an increase to the quarterly dividend to $0.825 per share. The dividend is payable December 11, 2023 to shareholders of record on November 16, 2023.</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">   </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Additionally,  the Board of Directors approved an incremental $5 billion share repurchase authorization. With the addition of this new authorization, the company has a total of $8.3 billion available under its share repurchase authorizations as of October 27.</font></div><div id="i577082ea0902489687fa8ebcb7144506_25"></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Strategic and Operations Update</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">At the Martinez Renewables LLC fuels facility, construction activities are progressing. Pretreatment capabilities are increasing through the second half of 2023, and the facility is expected to produce 730 million gallons per year by the end of 2023.</font></div><div><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">MPC&#8217;s Midstream segment remains focused on executing the strategic priorities of strict capital discipline, fostering a low-cost culture, and optimizing the portfolio. The company operates the nation&#8217;s largest refining system. MPC&#8217;s marketing system includes branded locations across the United States, including Marathon brand retail outlets. MPC also owns the general partner and majority limited partner interest in MPLX LP, a midstream company that owns and operates gathering, processing, and fractionation assets, as well as crude oil and light product transportation and logistics infrastructure. More information is available at www.marathonpetroleum.com.</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Investor Relations Contacts&#58; (419) 421-2071</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Kristina Kazarian, Vice President, Finance and Investor Relations</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Brian Worthington, Director, Investor Relations</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Kenan Kinsey, Supervisor, Investor Relations</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Media Contact&#58; (419) 421-3577</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Jamal Kheiry, Communications Manager </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div id="i577082ea0902489687fa8ebcb7144506_34"></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">References to Earnings and Defined Terms</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">References to earnings mean net income attributable to MPC from the statements of income. We believe excluding turnaround costs from this metric is useful for comparability to other companies as certain of our competitors defer these costs and amortize them between turnarounds. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Adjusted EBITDA is a financial performance measure used by management, industry analysts, investors, lenders, and rating agencies to assess the financial performance and operating results of our ongoing business operations. Additionally, we believe adjusted EBITDA provides useful information to investors for trending, analyzing and benchmarking our operating results from period to period as compared to other companies that may have different financing and capital structures. Adjusted EBITDA should not be considered as a substitute for, or superior to income (loss) from operations, net income attributable to MPC, income before income taxes, cash flows from operating activities or any other measure of financial performance presented in accordance with GAAP. Adjusted EBITDA may not be comparable to similarly titled measures reported by other companies.</font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div
